This is the best program to view your Point Of Interests (POI) files on offline map on your PC or phone.\r\nAfter select one of your POI you can start your desired Navigation program or another mapping program in your phone or PC. \r\nThe app supports different map style and color and it is GPS enabled to find your position. Cinebench scores are used by system administrators to help make purchase decisions, journalists to review hardware, hardware manufacturers to optimize their latest products, as well as computer owners to evaluate their individual system. \r\n\r\nImprovements to Cinebench Release 20 reflect the overall advancements to CPU and rendering technology in recent years, providing a more accurate measurement of Cinema 4D's ability to take advantage of multiple CPU cores and modern processor features available to the average user.\r\n\r\nCinebench R20 FAQs:\r\n\r\n•\tCinebench R20 uses a much larger and more complex test scene than R15 requiring about 8x the computational power needed to render it.
